\DoxyCodeLine{3643   JSON\_PRIVATE\_UNLESS\_TESTED:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644     \textcolor{comment}{// returns true if:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ any operand is NaN and the other operand is of number type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ any operand is discarded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647     \textcolor{comment}{// in legacy mode, discarded values are considered ordered if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648     \textcolor{comment}{// an operation is computed as an odd number of inverses of others}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} compares\_unordered(\mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac9d32cf719260c22b33bab670cd5602b}{const\_reference}} lhs, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac9d32cf719260c22b33bab670cd5602b}{const\_reference}} rhs, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} inverse = \textcolor{keyword}{false}) noexcept}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((lhs.is\_number\_float() \&\& std::isnan(lhs.m\_value.number\_float) \&\& rhs.is\_number())}

\DoxyCodeLine{3655         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if JSON\_USE\_LEGACY\_DISCARDED\_VALUE\_COMPARISON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (lhs.is\_discarded() || rhs.is\_discarded()) \&\& !inverse;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659         \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(inverse);}
